 poxo act ke tahat balaatkaar ke doshiyon ko nahin mili dayaa yachika kaa adhikarashtrapati ne sansad se dayaa yachika par punarvichaar karne kii apil kii hanaaballig bacchon ke saath hone vaale yon aparaadh main lagata he poxo actdesh main lagaataar ho rahe rape or hatya kii ghatnaon ko lekar janata main aakrosh ke bich raashtrapati ramnath kovind ne bada bayaan diya he
 President Kovind said that the convicts who rape children should not have any right to mercy petition
 shuukravaar ke rajasthan ke sirohi main ek kaarykram ke dauraan raashtrapati ne kaha, 'poxo (POCSO) act ke tahat balaatkaar ke doshiyon ko milane vaala dayaa yachika kaa adhikaar samaapt hona chahie
 "the President further said," The safety of women is a serious issue for the country
 poxo (POCSO) adhinium ke tahat balaatkaar ke doshiyon ko dayaa yachika daayar karne ke adhikaar se vanchit karnaa chahie
 Parliament should reconsider the mercy petition
 'kya hota he poxo (POCSO) act or sajaa?angreji shabd poxo kaa matlab hota he protection of children from sexual offences act 2012 (langik utpeedan se bacchon ke sangrakshan kaa adhinium 2012)
 Under this Act, action is taken in cases of sexual offenses and molestation occurring with minor children
 yah act bacchon ko sexual herracement, sexual asolt or pornography jaise gambhir aparaadhon se suraksha pradaan karata he
 Under this law enacted in the year 2012, the punishment has been fixed according to the crime
 jiskaa kadai se paalan kiya janaa bhi sunishchit kiya gaya he
 Cases under Section 4 of this Act include cases where the child has been raped or misdemeanor
 isamen saat saal karawas se lekar umrakaid or arthdand bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 Cases under Section 6 of the POCSO Act come in cases where children have been severely hurt after rape or misdemeanor
 isamen das saal karawas se umrakaid tak kii sajaa ho sakati he or jurmaana bhi lagaaya ja saktaa he
 Similarly, under sections 7 and 8 of the Poxo Act, cases are registered in which the children's genitals are molested
 is dhara main aropiyon par dosha siddh hone par paanch se saat saal tak kii sajaa or jurmaana hota he
 Penetrative sexual assault is also defined under Section 3 of the Poxo Act
 jisamen bachche ke sharir ke saath kisi bhi tarah kii harakat karne vaale shaks ko kadi sajaa kaa praavdhaan he
 Any kind of sexual behavior from children under 18 years of age comes under the purview of this law
 yah kanoon ladke or ladki ko samaan rup se suraksha pradaan karata he
 The cases to be registered under this law are heard in a special court

 jaise-taise use aspataal pahunchaaya jaataa he, jahaan philhal uski jaan batch gai

 main jaananaa chahta tha ki agar wo mujhe bahut pyaar karti he to mujhe peeche khinch legi

 'pan ko sir or chaati par kaaphi fracture aae hai
